;------  Ancillaries: Scripts  ----------------------------;ancillaries tied to a script

;------  Ancillaries: Armours  ----------------------------

;------  Triggers: Next Heir  -----------------------------

Trigger stewards_seal
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition IsFactionHeir
        and FactionIsLocal
        and FactionType sicily
        and not FactionwideAncillaryExists stewards_seal

    AcquireAncillary stewards_seal chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------

    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

;------  Triggers: Pets & Animals  ------------------------
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger Crebain_Add1
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement

    Condition FactionType france
        and IsGeneral
        and not HasAncType pet
        and SettlementName Nan_Curunir
        and TimeInRegion >= 4

    AcquireAncillary crebain Chance 2
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger Crebain_Add2
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition IsRegionOneOf 98 102 117 ; Dunland-Hills_Province Dunland_Province Duneard_Province
        and FactionType aztecs
        and IsGeneral
        and not HasAncType pet
        and CharacterAge >= 40
        and TimeInRegion >= 4

    AcquireAncillary crebain Chance 3
;----------------------------------------------------------

        and Attribute Loyalty > 4

Trigger gain_ring_end
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition Trait TemporaryRingTrait > 0
    and not I_WorldwideAncillaryExists one_ring
    and I_EventCounter ring_transfer = 0

    AcquireAncillary one_ring Chance  100
;----------------------------------------------------------      
Trigger ringtrait_remove_general
    WhenToTest GeneralPrisonersRansomedCaptive 

    Condition Trait TemporaryRingTrait > 0
    and I_WorldwideAncillaryExists one_ring
    
    Affects TemporaryRingTrait  -1  Chance  100
;----------------------------------------------------------     
Trigger ringtrait_remove_sack
    WhenToTest SackSettlement  

    Condition Trait TemporaryRingTrait > 0
    and I_WorldwideAncillaryExists one_ring
    
    Affects TemporaryRingTrait  -1  Chance  100
;----------------------------------------------------------     
Trigger ringtrait_remove_exterminate
    WhenToTest ExterminatePopulation  

    Condition Trait TemporaryRingTrait > 0
    and I_WorldwideAncillaryExists one_ring
    
    Affects TemporaryRingTrait  -1  Chance  100
;----------------------------------------------------------     
Trigger ringtrait_remove_occupy
    WhenToTest OccupySettlement  

    Condition Trait TemporaryRingTrait > 0
    and I_WorldwideAncillaryExists one_ring
    
    Affects TemporaryRingTrait  -1  Chance  100
;----------------------------------------------------------  
Trigger ringtrait_remove_multiturnmove
    WhenToTest MultiTurnMove  

    Condition Trait TemporaryRingTrait > 0
    and I_WorldwideAncillaryExists one_ring
    
    Affects TemporaryRingTrait  -1  Chance  100
;----------------------------------------------------------

    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd  

    Condition Trait TemporaryRingTrait > 0
    
    Affects TemporaryRingTrait  -1  Chance  100
